line=398 tag=M:     5 Sometimes the verb that vegig in its object-related interpretation combines with differs
line=399 tag=B:                                    ´
line=400 tag=M:  in selectional restrictions from the resulting combination. In such cases a greater or lesser
line=401 tag=M:  degree of lexicalization is at work. For example, although the verb visz (the infinitive is
line=402 tag=M:  vinni) `take' in (13) is transitive, without vegig it cannot take an event-denoting noun phrase
line=403 tag=B:                                                ´
line=404 tag=M:  (e.g. maganos´ as `privativization') as its object. See footnote 6 for another example.
